    |    Variance = SumSq / N = 280.378579 / 100 = 2.803786
    |    Global Cost = 2.803786
    |    Weighted Global = (1 - alpha - beta) * Global Cost
    |                    = (1 - 0.00 - 0.00) * 2.803786
    |                    = 1.00 * 2.803786 = 2.803786

    |    Global Discomfort Sum = Sum(LocalCost_i) for all agents i

    |    Global Discomfort Sum = 3.000000
    |    Num Agents = 4

    |               = 3.000000 / 4 = 0.750000
    |    Weighted Local = beta * Local Cost
    |                   = 0.00 * 0.750000 = 0.000000
    |
    | 3. Unfairness Calculation (Standard Deviation of Discomfort):
    |    Global Discomfort Sum Sqr = 3.000000
    |    E[X^2] = SumSqr / N = 3.000000 / 4 = 0.750000
    |    (E[X])^2 = (Sum / N)^2 = (3.000000 / 4)^2 = 0.562500

    |    Weighted Unfairness = alpha * Unfairness
